Chants, the beating of sticks and shouts fill the air. </p><p class="Text-sc-1amvtpj-0-p render-stellar-contentstyles__Paragraph-sc-9v7nwy-2 fAchMW"><strong>Civilians caught in the mix: </strong>Meanwhile, passersby are trying to get home, but find themselves blocked by the protesters and police.
